    <script type="text/javascript">
      function getStars(rating) {
        console.log('getStarrs' + R);

        // Round to nearest half
        rating = Math.round(rating * 2) / 2;
        console.log('rating' + rating);
        let output = [];

        // Append all the filled whole stars
        for (var i = rating; i >= 1; i--)
          output.push('<i class="fa fa-star custom-star" aria-hidden="true""></i>&nbsp;');

        // If there is a half a star, append it
        if (i == .5)
          output.push('<i class="fa fa-star-half-o custom-star" aria-hidden="true"></i>&nbsp;');

        // Fill the empty stars
        for (let i = (5 - rating); i >= 1; i--)
          output.push('<i class="fa fa-star-o custom-star" aria-hidden="true"></i>&nbsp;');

        return output.join('');

      }
    </script>

<script>
function getCookie(name) {
    var dc = document.cookie;
    var prefix = name + "=";
    var begin = dc.indexOf("; " + prefix);
    if (begin == -1) {
        begin = dc.indexOf(prefix);
        if (begin != 0) return null;
    }
    else
    {
        begin += 2;
        var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
        if (end == -1) {
        end = dc.length;
        }
    }
    // because unescape has been deprecated, replaced with decodeURI
    //return unescape(dc.substring(begin + prefix.length, end));
    return decodeURI(dc.substring(begin + prefix.length, end));
} 

function setCookie(name,value,days) {
    var expires = "";
    if (days) {
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));
        expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
    }
    document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "")  + expires + "; path=/";
}

function showConsent() {
    var myCookie = getCookie("consent_State");
    var consent_Box = document.getElementById("consentBox");
    if (myCookie == null) {
        // do cookie doesn't exist stuff;
        
        consent_Box.style.display = "block";
    }
    else {
        consent_Box.style.display = "none";
        gtag('consent', 'update', {
      'ad_storage': 'granted',
      'ad_user_data': 'granted',
      'ad_personalization': 'granted',
      'analytics_storage': 'granted',
      'functionality_storage': 'granted',
      'personalization_storage': 'granted',
      'security_storage': 'granted'
    });
        // do cookie exists stuff
    }
}


setTimeout(showConsent, 6000);




 // Define dataLayer and the gtag function.
 window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
  function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}




function grant_consent(){
//const updateConsentState = require('updateConsentState');
gtag('consent', 'update', {
      'ad_storage': 'granted',
      'ad_user_data': 'granted',
      'ad_personalization': 'granted',
      'analytics_storage': 'granted',
      'functionality_storage': 'granted',
      'personalization_storage': 'granted',
      'security_storage': 'granted'
    });
// updateConsentState({
//   'ad_storage': 'granted',
//   'ad_user_data': 'granted',
//   'ad_personalization': 'granted',
//   'analytics_storage': 'granted',
//   'functionality_storage': 'granted',
//   'personalization_storage': 'granted',
//   'security_storage': 'granted'
// });
setCookie("consent_State","true",365);
var consent_Box = document.getElementById("consentBox");
consent_Box.style.display = "none";

}
</script>

    <script>
        function youTubes_makeDynamic() {
            var $ytIframes = $('iframe[src*="youtube.com"]');
            $ytIframes.each(function(i, e) {
                var $ytFrame = $(e);
                var ytKey;
                var tmp = $ytFrame.attr('src').split(/\//);
                tmp = tmp[tmp.length - 1];
                tmp = tmp.split('?');
                ytKey = tmp[0];
                var $ytLoader = $('<div>');
                $ytLoader.append($('<img class="cover cover1 aligncenter" src="https://i.ytimg.com/vi/' + ytKey + '/hqdefault.jpg">'));
                $ytLoader.append($('<img class="icn-img" style="position: absolute;z-index: 2; top: 0 !important; left: 0 !important; bottom: 0 !important; right: 0 !important; display: block !important; margin: auto !important; cursor: pointer;" src="https://img.icons8.com/color/60/000000/youtube-play.png">'));
                $ytLoader.data('$ytFrame', $ytFrame);
                $ytFrame.replaceWith($ytLoader);
                $ytLoader.click(function() {
                    var $ytFrame = $ytLoader.data('$ytFrame');
                    $ytFrame.attr('src', $ytFrame.attr('src') + '?autoplay=1');
                    $ytLoader.replaceWith($ytFrame);
                });
            });
        };
        $(document).ready(function() {
            youTubes_makeDynamic()
        });
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function focus() {
        document.getElementById("sub_email").autofocus = true;
    }
    var count = 0;

    if(window.location.href != 'https://www.dailymusicroll.com/'){

    jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
        var scrollPos = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )NewsletterForm=([^;]+)'));
        if (match) {
            var oldCookie = match[2];
            //console.log("COOKIS", oldCookie);
        } else {
            //console.log('--something went wrong---');
            var oldCookie = 'blank'
        }
        if (scrollPos >= 500 && count < 1 && oldCookie == 'blank') {
            //console.log("open_new_modal");
           // open_new_modal();
            count++;
        }
    });

    }

    function modalSubmit(e) {
        //console.log(e)
        const sub_username = document.getElementById("sub_username").value;
        const sub_email = document.getElementById("sub_email").value;
        const ajaxurl = window.location.href;
        const url = window.location.href;
        const cate = "0";
        const timeperiod = "daily";

        //console.log(sub_username);

        $.ajax({
            url: "https://www.dailymusicroll.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
            // url:ajaxurl,
            type: 'post',
            async: true,
            data: {
                action: 'sub',
                name: sub_username,
                email: sub_email,
                cate: cate,
                url: url,
                timeperiod: timeperiod
            },
            error: function(response) {
                //console.log(response);
            },
            success: function(response) {
                //console.log(response);

                const error = document.getElementById("error");
                while (error.firstChild) {
                    error.removeChild(error.lastChild);
                }
                error.append(`${response}`);
                if (response.trim() == "Subscribed") {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        close_new_modal();
                    }, 2000);


                    var date = new Date();
                    var hours = 24;
                    date.setTime(+date + (hours * 3600000));
                    //console.log(date.toGMTString());
                    document.cookie = `NewsletterForm=yes; expires=${date.toGMTString()}; path=/`;

                }

            }
        });

    }

    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

        $('select[multiple].active.3col').multiselect({

                'default': 'Search Category'

        $("#subbtn").click(function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var sub_name = $('#sub_username1').val();
            var sub_email = $('#sub_email1').val();
            var ajaxurl = $(this).attr('url');
            var cate = $('#category').val();
            var timeperiod = $("input[name=timeperiod]:checked").val();
            var url = window.location.href;
            //console.log(sub_email);
            $.ajax({
                url: "https://www.dailymusicroll.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
                type: 'post',
                async: true,
                data: {
                    action: 'sub',
                    name: sub_name,
                    email: sub_email,
                    cate: cate,
                    url: url,
                    timeperiod: timeperiod
                },
                error: function(response) {
                    //console.log(response);
                },
                success: function(response) {
                    //console.log(response);
                    $("#error").children().remove();
                    $("#error").append(`<p>${response}</p>`);
                    if (response == "Subscribed") {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            close_new_modal();
                        }, 2000);


                        var date = new Date();
                        var hours = 24;
                        date.setTime(+date + (hours * 3600000));
                        //console.log(date.toGMTString());
                        document.cookie = `NewsletterForm=yes; expires=${date.toGMTString()}; path=/`;

                    }

                }
            });
        });


        $('#newsLetterSignupBtn').click(function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var uN = "Demo";
            var uE = jQuery("#newsLetterSignupEmail").val().trim();
            var catIdString = "00";
            var catNameString = "home";
            var url = window.location.href;
            var sub_name = "admin";
            var timeperiod = "weekly";
            var cate = "00";

            //console.log(uE);
            if (uN == "" || uN.indexOf(" ") == 0) {

                document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "Name is required!";
                //console.log("Name is required!");
            } else {
                document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "";

                if (uE == "" || uE.indexOf(" ") == 0) {
                    document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "Email is required!";
                    //console.log("Email is required!");
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "";
                    }, 5000);

                } else if (uE.indexOf("@") <= 0 || uE.indexOf("@") >= uE.length - 1) {
                    document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "Please enter valid email!";
                    //console.log("Please enter valid email!");
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "";
                    }, 5000);

                } else if (uE.charAt(uE.length - 4) != "." && uE.charAt(uE.length - 3) != ".") {
                    document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "Email is badly formatted!";
                    //console.log("Email is badly formatted!");
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "";
                    }, 5000);

                } else {
                    document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "";
                    $.ajax({
                        url: "https://www.dailymusicroll.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
                        type: 'post',
                        async: true,
                        data: {
                            action: 'sub',
                            name: sub_name,
                            email: uE,
                            cate: cate,
                            url: url,
                            timeperiod: timeperiod
                        },
                        success: function(response) {
                            //console.log(response)
                            if (response.trim() == 'Subscribed') {
                                jQuery("#newsLetterSignupEmail").val("");
                                document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "Thanks for Subscribed! ";
                            } else {
                                document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "oops! It seems you have already subscribed to Daily Newsletters.";
                            }

                            setTimeout(() => {
                                document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "";
                            }, 5000);
                        },
                        error: function(response) {
                            //console.log(response);

                        },
                    });

                }
            } //end if

        }); //

        $('#newslatter-btn').click(function(e) {

            e.preventDefault();
            var uN = "Demo";
            var uE = $(this).siblings('#email-signup').val().trim();
            var catIdString = "00";
            var catNameString = "home";
            var url = window.location.href;
            var sub_name = "admin";
            var timeperiod = "weekly";
            var cate = "00";

            //console.log(uE);
            if (uN == "" || uN.indexOf(" ") == 0) {

                $(this).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("Name is required!");
                // //console.log("Name is required!");
            } else {
                $(this).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("");

                if (uE == "" || uE.indexOf(" ") == 0) {

                    $(this).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("Email is required!");

                    //console.log("Email is required!");
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        $(this).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("");

                    }, 5000);

                } else if (uE.indexOf("@") <= 0 || uE.indexOf("@") >= uE.length - 1) {

                    $(this).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("Please enter valid email!");

                    //console.log("Please enter valid email!");
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        $(this).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("");
                    }, 5000);

                } else if (uE.charAt(uE.length - 4) != "." && uE.charAt(uE.length - 3) != ".") {
                    $(this).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("Email is badly formatted!");
                    //console.log("Email is badly formatted!");
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        document.getElementById("newsLetterSignupError").innerHTML = "";
                        $(this).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("");
                    }, 5000);

                } else {

                    $(this).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("");
                    var obj = this;
                    $.ajax({
                        url: "https://www.dailymusicroll.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
                        type: 'post',
                        async: true,
                        data: {
                            action: 'sub',
                            name: sub_name,
                            email: uE,
                            cate: cate,
                            url: url,
                            timeperiod: timeperiod
                        },
                        success: function(response) {
                            //console.log(response)
                            if (response.trim() == 'Subscribed') {
                                jQuery("#newsLetterSignupEmail").val("");
                                $(obj).siblings("#email-signup").val("");
                                $(obj).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("Thanks for Subscribed! ");
                            } else {
                                $(obj).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("oops! It seems you have already subscribed to Daily Newsletters.");
                            }

                            setTimeout(() => {
                                $(obj).parents(".newslatter_form").siblings(".error").text("");

                            }, 5000);
                        },
                        error: function(response) {
                            //console.log(response);

                        },
                    });

                }
            } //end if

        });

    });

    function openDIV() {

        document.getElementById("myDIV").style.WebkitTransitionTimingFunction = "cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55)"; // Safari 3.1 to 6.0
        document.getElementById("myDIV").style.TransitionTimingFunction = "cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55)";

        document.getElementById("myDIV").style.visibility = "visible";

        jQuery("#myDIV").addClass("DIVShow");
        jQuery("#myDIV").removeClass("DIVHide");

        jQuery("#crossBtn").removeClass("divCrossButtonClick");


        document.getElementById("newsLetter1").style.display = "none";
        document.getElementById("newsLetter11").style.display = "block";
        document.getElementById("paraSub1").style.display = "none";
        document.getElementById("paraSub3").style.display = "none";
        document.getElementById("paraSub2").style.display = "block";
        document.getElementById("paraSub4").style.display = "block";


    }

    function closeDIV() {

        document.getElementById("myDIV").style.TransitionTimingFunction = "cubic-bezier(0.25, 0.46, 0.45, 0.94) ";
        document.getElementById("myDIV").style.WebkitTransitionTimingFunction = "cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55)"; // Safari 3.1 to 6.0

        document.getElementById("myDIV").style.visibility = "hidden";

        jQuery("#myDIV").addClass("DIVHide");
        jQuery("#crossBtn").addClass("divCrossButtonClick"); //to rotate the close button on click

        jQuery("#myDIV").removeClass("DIVShow");
        jQuery("#uName").removeClass("inputField");
        jQuery("#uEmail").removeClass("inputField");

        jQuery("#uName").val("");
        jQuery("#uEmail").val("");
        jQuery("#name_info").text("");

        var date = new Date();
        var hours = 24;
        date.setTime(+date + (hours * 3600000));
        //console.log(date.toGMTString());
        document.cookie = `NewsletterForm=yes; expires=${date.toGMTString()}; path=/`;

    }

    function open_new_modal() {
        const modal = document.getElementById("customModal");
        // var mainpage = document.getElementById("vl-page");
        // var footer = document.getElementById("vl-colophon");

        // mainpage.style.opacity = "0.3";
        // footer.style.opacity = "0.3";

        $('#vl-page').addClass('customPopupBg');
        $('#vl-colophon').addClass('customPopupBg');


        modal.style.display = "block";

        $.ajax({
            url: "https://www.dailymusicroll.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
            type: 'post',
            dataType: 'text',
            data: {
                action: 'modal_display'
            },
            error: function(response) {
                //console.log(response);
            },
            success: function(response) {
                $('#customModal').html(response);
            }
        })
    }

    function email_subscription() {
        event.preventDefault();
        var sub_email = $('#sub_email').val();
        $('#subscribeButton').prop('disabled', true);
        $.ajax({
            url: "https://www.dailymusicroll.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
            type: 'post',
            // dataType: 'text',
            data: {
                action: 'sub',
                email: sub_email
            },
            error: function(response) {
                //console.log(response);
            },
            success: function(response) {
                var html = response;
                $('#error').html(html);
                if(response != "Subscribed"){
                    $('#subscribeButton').prop('disabled', false);
                }else{
                setTimeout(() => {
                    $('#customModal').hide();
                    $('#vl-page').removeClass('customPopupBg');
                    $('#vl-colophon').removeClass('customPopupBg');
                }, 3000);
                }
            }
        })
    }

    function close_new_modal() {
        // const sub_username = document.getElementById("sub_username1");
        // sub_username.value = "";
        const sub_email = document.getElementById("sub_email");
        sub_email.value = "";
        const error = document.getElementById("error");
        while (error.firstChild) {
            error.removeChild(error.lastChild);
        }

        $("#modal_content").children().remove();

        $('#vl-page').removeClass('customPopupBg');
        $('#vl-colophon').removeClass('customPopupBg');

        var modal = document.getElementById("customModal");
        modal.style.display = "none";

        var date = new Date();
        var hours = 48;
        date.setTime(+date + (hours * 3600000));
        //console.log(date.toGMTString());
        document.cookie = `NewsletterForm=yes; expires=${date.toGMTString()}; path=/`;
    }

    function subscribed_user(id) {
        var sub_email = $(`#email${id}`).val();
        $.ajax({
            url: "https://www.dailymusicroll.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
            type: 'post',
            data: {
                action: 'sub',
                email: sub_email
            },
            error: function(response) {
                //console.log(response);
            },
            success: function(response) {
                var html = response;
                $(`#message${id}`).append(html);
                // setTimeout(() => {
                //     $("#modal_content").children().remove();
                // }, 3000); 
            }
        });
    }
</script>


</body>
